<userid>104600150006171765694<//userid>< user_name>
Sam Khandelwal</user_name>
<time>1605253856349<//time><rating>3</rating><review>3/5

Friendly staff. Easy pickup experience.

Perhaps the Bay Area and the recent trip to Israel has spoilt me with excellent falafel plates and falafel sandwiches. I was excited to try Pita Pockets, especially after reading the excellent reviews.

My experience was average. The falafel was slightly soggy, lacked the crisp/crunchy texture and did not have a distinct flavor.

The falafel plate had plain boiled white rice, which lacked flavor or seasoning.

Perhaps, the food is better enjoyed fresh at the restaurant than as takeout. Also, this place may be better for their meat options. Or they were having an off day.

It's COVID, and restaurants are working very hard, so I do not want to dissuade anyone from giving Pita Pockets a shot. I did, and found them lacking, but this is purely based on the 2 falafel items that I experienced.

On the positive side, their hummus wasn't bad. Also, they have a hot sauce that I enjoyed -- it adds a much needed punch to your falafel sandwich.</review>< Pics>

< rating>
5<//rating>
<review>There is nothing I can say about this place that everyone in Northridge doesn't already know. Family run business, fresh food, and laffa bread made right when you order it. You haven't had laffa bread before? Then please try it here first. Allow your first experience with this deliciousness to be at a place that has perfected it.

I have been ordering the same thing every time I come here since they first opened...Chicken Shawarma Laffa. Think of it like a mediterranean burrito. You can call it a wrap, but it isn't remotely close to what most people envision when they hear the word wrap. The chicken shawarma is rotating slowly on a vertical rotisserie waiting to be placed in the the warm laffa. You get a choice of fries or rice. Not on the side, but on the inside of your laffa creation. Go with the fries. Trust me. They top it off with hummus, lettuce, tomatoes and marinated onions and roll it up like what could only be described as a giant burrito.

I have been all over Los Angeles and tried shawarma and laffa at dozens of places. Pita Pockets is the best. Hands down.< /review>< Pics>

< review>
DELICIOUS! I got the Chicken Shawarma Laffa, which was so big I couldn't even finish it. They gave me some extra foil to wrap it up, and I got to enjoy the rest of it for lunch the next day. My friend devoured the Gyro Plate (except for what I was able to sample!) The meat practically melted in your mouth, it was so tasty and spiced to perfection. The hummus was fresh and the pita - just WOW! So soft, warm and flavorful.

I was surprised that we were the only ones in this little gem of a restaurant. I will definitely be back to try everything else on the menu!<//review>

< review>
This was my first time there, though I had been meaning to go for awhile. I love falafel pitas so I finally went to Pita Pockets to get one. Disaster. My first mistake was being talked into using laffa bread instead of the usual pita bread. The laffa bread was not fluffy, only thick, very dry and rough. Then there was only maybe a teaspoon of sauce on the sandwich along with a scant amount of shredded carrot  and lettuce, however the supreme
Insult were the falafel balls themselves. Omg, they were not fried, they were mealy, a bit slimy and had absolutely no flavor whatsoever! I only give 1 star to this place because it was clean and the counter person that I dealt with was very friendly. I will never go back to Pita Pockets.<//review>

<rate>4</rate>< Review>
This place is a gem. The laffa gyro is huge and stuffed with great tasty ingredients. It costs a bit more than the pita but It's more like a burrito and very large in size.

The feta fries are quite good too. The feta is super smooth, not crumbly.

The staff is very friendly.

They have a Coke soda fountain here too.

While I did enjoy the gyro, I do want to try the falafel next time.

My only gripe is that the seating is mostly 2 person only. You also have the patio which can accommodate more, but is limited.</Review>

< Review>
We ate here recently while visiting SD as it was close to our hotel on a rainy cold night. What a lovely experience--very romantic! The restaurant is absolutely beautiful, and our meal was so delicious! We shared a scrumptious salad and the lasagna was surely the best we have ever tasted. There are many restaurants in SD, but we will definitely have to return here on our next visit! for dessert, I got some kind of cherry cheesecake and it was to die for. I can't remember what my friend got for dessert because I was so enraptured by mine!<//Review>

< Review>
This review is for the coffee shop part.

This is true espresso bar with great quality. I enjoy lighter/medium roast espressos and they have that. They took extra care for making a shot with good solid crema. I recommend this for espressos and keep going back.

The staff was welcoming and well serving.

There are enough of outside seating.

They down side that they close the espresso bar before they close the skate board side. If shop was to close at 6pm then bar closed 3:20pm already. The store hours does not reflect that and could make a trip that does not end with great cup of espresso.</Review>

< Review>
Awesome central location skate shop on this spot for more than 20 years. Decks & all the gear you need as well as shoes, clothes, caps skate apparel too.

Great coffee at the adjacent shop  with compostable cups & lids, cool pics on the walls and lots of natural light from the big glass windows everywhere.

Interesting health and #sustainability feature is that there's no dairy milk on offer only oat or  almond milk if needed with coffee. #vegan #plantbased

So much nicer to buy gear and coffee here than inside a shopping mall.</Review>

<userid>113137489682074618788<//userid>< Review>
I ordered a carnitas burrito,  with no extras and it totaled $10 and some change. I was excited because of the positive rating on Google but what I got was less than exciting. The burrito was very small the sour cream and guacamole that was supposed to be inside was instead served on the side. as you can see in the pic,  my first bite was extremely unpleasant. There was what I can best describe as a wooden branch about 2.5 inches long inside my burrito. It was too hard to be a tomato vine - hard enough to hurt my mouth when I bit into it. After thoroughly checking the rest of the burrito I decided to continue eating. The tortilla was really good,  however the only other contents were rice (I ordered no beans)  meat and a few pieces of tomato. The carnitas was extremely salty and nothing else had any flavor. I asked for hot salsa,  which might have saved the meal in terms of flavor,  but none was given. I've had $5 taco truck burritos that were 10 times better. The price matched with the quality of the product means I'll likely not try this restaurant again. If you do, beware of foreign objects and make sure you get what you asked for. Good luck!< /Review>
